# Papaen IELTS Speaking Part 2&3 Archive

- Topic count: 682
- Question count: 4062
- Source version: 6745
- Exported at: 2026-07-07T09:31:32.676Z

## 1. 发小 / 人物 / NEW
1. [Part 2] Describe a friend from your childhood You should say: Who he/she is Where you met each other What you often did together And explain what made you like him/her
2. [Part 3] What do you think of online social media?
3. [Part 3] Do you still keep in touch with your friends from childhood? Why or why not?
4. [Part 3] How important is childhood friendship to children?
5. [Part 3] What do you think of communicating via social media?
6. [Part 3] Do you use a lot of emojis online?
7. [Part 3] Do you think online communication through social media will replace face-to-face communication?

## 2. 交通拥堵 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 2] Describe a time when you were stuck in a traffic jam You should say: When it happened Where you were stuck What you did while waiting And explain how you felt in the traffic jam
2. [Part 3] How can we solve the traffic jam problem?
3. [Part 3] Do you think developing public transportation can solve traffic jam problems?
4. [Part 3] Do you think highways can help reduce traffic jams?
5. [Part 3] What are some effective ways to manage traffic?
6. [Part 3] Would you rather be in a car or a bus in a traffic jam?
7. [Part 3] Do you like to use public transport?

## 3. 语言学习 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 2] Describe something that helped you learn a language You should say What it is What language you learned How it helped you learn the language And how you felt about it
2. [Part 3] What difficulties do people face when learning a language?
3. [Part 3] Do you think language learning is important? Why?
4. [Part 3] Which is better, to study alone or to study in a group? Why?
5. [Part 3] What’s the best way to learn a language?

## 4. 收到特殊蛋糕 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 2] Describe a special cake you received from others You should say When it happened Where it happened Who you got the cake from And explain why it’s a special cake
2. [Part 3] Do you think it’s good to communicate when eating with your family?
3. [Part 3] Why are some people willing to spend a lot of money on meals or special days?
4. [Part 3] Is there any food in your country that is eaten at special times or on special occasions?
5. [Part 3] What are the difference between special food in China and foreign countries?
6. [Part 3] In your country, do people nowadays cook at home as frequently as people did in the past?
7. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do people usually cook special food in China?

## 5. 重要河流/湖泊 / 事物 / NEW
1. [Part 2] Describe an important river/lake in your country You should say: Where it is located How big/long it is What it looks like And explain why it is important
2. [Part 3] How can rivers/lakes benefit local people?
3. [Part 3] Do you think rivers/lakes attract tourists?
4. [Part 3] How do rivers and lakes affect local tourism?
5. [Part 3] Are rivers and lakes good for transport?
6. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think rivers and lakes attract tourists?
7. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do people in your country go swimming in their spare time?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Is it necessary for everyone to learn swimming?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do people like the rivers in your country?

## 6. 花费甚少的外出日 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 2] Describe a special day out that cost you little money/didn’t cost you much You should say: When was the day Where you went How much you spent And explain how you feel about the day
2. [Part 3] Do people like to spend their leisure time outside in your country?
3. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How do people spend their leisure time in China?
4. [Part 3] How does technology affect the way people spend their leisure time?

7. [Part 3] Why do people like to have days off?
8. [Part 3] How do people spend their leisure time in your country?

11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Have you ever had a bad shopping experience?
12. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How can people save as much money as possible?
13. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do teenagers spend more money than they used to?

## 9. 包含动物的故事或书 / 事物 / NEW

## 10. 很久没收到回复的信息 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 2] Describe a time when you sent a message or anemail to someone but received no reply for a longtime You should say: Who you sent it to What the message/email was about Whether you finally received the reply And explain how you felt about the experience
2. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Why do some people feel angry when others don't reply to their message?
3. [Part 3] How do you show your respect in your messages?

6. [Part 3] In what situations do people not respond to messages at all?
7. [Part 3] In what situations do people spend a long time responding to others' messages?

## 11. 组织快乐活动 / 事件 / NEW

## 670. 他城的短暂停留 / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe another city you would like to stay for a short time You should say: Where the city is Why you want to go there Whom you will go there with What you will do there And explain why you will stay there just for a short time
2. [Part 3] Why do many people like to travel abroad?
3. [Part 3] Why do places with historical sites develop tourism industry more actively?
4. [Part 3] Why is the noise pollution worse in tourism cities than in other cities?
5. [Part 3] Do most people like planned traveling?
6. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think there will be more ecotourism in the future?
7. [Part 3] Do you think tourists may come across bad things in other cities?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What do people usually do during long holidays?
9. [Part 3] Why do people sometimes go to other cities?
10. [Part 3] Why are historical cities popular?
11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What are some popular attractions that people like to visit?

## 671. 擅长外语的人 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Is learning a foreign language important?
2. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What benefits can a foreign language bring to one’s career?
3. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think English will be the mainstream of the world in the future?
4. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] When learning a foreign language, which part is easier? Speaking or writing?

## 672. 【低频】教他人做事 / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe a time when you taught a friend/relative something You should say: Who you taught What you taught What the result was And explain how you felt about the experience
2. [Part 3] How can we know what to do when we want to learn something new?
3. [Part 3] How can young people teach old people skills?
4. [Part 3] What skills can young people teach old people besides technology?
5. [Part 3] What practical skills can young people teach old people?
6. [Part 3] Do people in your country like to watch videos to learn something?
7. [Part 3] Do you think 'showing' is a better way than 'telling' in education?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What skills should be taught to children?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What skills do adults need to have？
10. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What can children learn from teachers and parents?
11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What are the skills that you wanted to learn?
12. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How can people be motivated to learn new things？

## 673. 【疑似淘汰】有趣的老人 / 人物 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe an interesting old person you met You should say: Who this person is When/where you met this person What you did with this person And explain why you think this person is interesting
2. [Part 3] What benefits can people get if they are self-centered?
3. [Part 3] Do you think people are more selfish or self-centered now than in the past?
4. [Part 3] Are there benefits when one person is interested in another person? Why?
5. [Part 3] Is it easy for young people and old people to make friends with each other?
6. [Part 3] Do you think old people and young people can share interests?
7. [Part 3] What can old people teach young people?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think old people should live with their family?

## 674. 和别人一起做的事【海外】 / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe something that you did with someone/a group of people You should say: What it was Who you did it with How long it took you to do this And explain why you did it together
2. [Part 3] Do you think it's important for children to learn about cooperation?
3. [Part 3] Do you think parents should teach children how to cooperate with others? How?
4. [Part 3] How do children learn to cooperate with each other?
5. [Part 3] Do you think neighbors help each other more often in the countryside than in the city?
6. [Part 3] How do neighbors help each other?
7. [Part 3] How do you get along with your neighbors?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What kinds of people do you like to work with?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think managers can be friends with their subordinates?
10. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Which one is more important to you at work, development in work related skills or the recognition from your supervisors?

## 675. 感兴趣的历史时期 / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe a historical period you would like to know more You should say: When it happened What you are interested in What you have known And explain why you would like to know more
2. [Part 3] Who should pay for the preservation of historic buildings?
3. [Part 3] Who should be responsible for protecting historic buildings?
4. [Part 3] Is it difficult to protect and preserve historic buildings?
5. [Part 3] What are the differences between learning history from books and videos?
6. [Part 3] In what ways can children learn history?
7. [Part 3] Should everyone know history?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What’s the difference between the history taught in primary school and the history taught in high school?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How do you learn history?
10. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Why do some people have no interest in history?
11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How can we protect old buildings?

## 676. 投诉并得到满意结果 / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe a complaint that you were satisfied with the result. You should say: Who you complained to What you complained about When it happened And explain why you were satisfied with the result
2. [Part 3] How do people often respond to poor customer service?
3. [Part 3] How would you react if you received a poor service at a restaurant?
4. [Part 3] What do people often complain about?
5. [Part 3] When are people more likely to make complaints?
6. [Part 3] Who are more likely to make complaints, older people or younger people?
7. [Part 3] Which one is better when making a complaint, by talking or by writing?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What products or services do people in your country like to complain about?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think customers’ complaints will improve products or services?
10. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Is it necessary for companies to set up customer service?
11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Are there any disadvantages to set up customer service?
12. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Would you buy things in the shops which you have made complaints before?

## 677. 童年喜欢的活动（疑似淘汰） / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2 / HIDDEN] Describe an activity you enjoyed your free time when you were young You should say: What it was Where you did it Who you did it with And explain why you enjoyed it
2. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Are there more activities for young people now than 20 years ago?
3. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What sports do young people like to do now?
4. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Is it important to have a break during work or study?
5. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do adults and children have enough time for leisure activities nowadays?
6. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What activities do children and adults do nowadays?
7. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Can most people balance work and life in China?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think winning is the most important goal for playing games?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do parents in your country encourage children to play games?
10. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Why do people play different kinds of games when they grow up?
11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What kinds of games do children play these days?

## 678. 聚会上遇到的人 / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe a person you met at a party who you enjoyed talking with You should say: What party it was Who the person is What you talked about And explain why you enjoyed talking with him/her
2. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think people can make more friends if they often attend parties?
3. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Should parents spend a lot of money on their children's birthday parties?
4. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do Chinese people like to hold parties?
5. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What do adults do at parties?
6. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What do children often do in a birthday party?
7. [Part 3] Is it difficult for adults to talk to children?
8. [Part 3] Why are some people unwilling to have conversations with other people?
9. [Part 3] Is it difficult for Chinese people to communicate with people from other countries?
10. [Part 3] How do people start a conversation?
11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Where would people get to know new people?
12. [Part 3] Where can people go to meet new people?
13. [Part 3] On what occasions would people be willing to get to know new people?

## 680. 不寻常的一餐 / 事件
1. [Part 2] Describe an unusual meal you had You should say： When you had it Where you had it Whom you had it with And explain why it was unusual
2. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think people are less willing to cook meals by themselves these days，compared to the past？
3. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What do you think are the benefits of having dinner together？
4. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do young people like to spend time with their families or friends？
5. [Part 3] Do you think having dinner at home is a good idea？
6. [Part 3] What are the advantages and disadvantages of eating in restaurants?
7. [Part 3] Do people in your country value food culture?
8. [Part 3] Do people in your country socialize in restaurants? Why?
9. [Part 3] Why do people choose to eat out instead of ordering takeout?
10. [Part 3] Do people eat fast food at home?
11. [Part 3] What fast food is there in your country?

## 681. 【低频】好消息 / 事件 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe a piece of good news that you heard about someone you know well You should say: What it was When you heard it How you knew it And explain how you felt about it
2. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What do you think of the news on social media?
3. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How can companies share news with the public? On the internet or through press conferences?
4. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Where do people get news?
5. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How do people share good news?
6. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] How does modern technology affect the delivery of information?
7. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] When do people share good news?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What sort of good news have you received?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What kinds of good news do people like to hear?
10. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Why do some people share news on social media?
11. [Part 3] Do people like to hear good news from their friends?
12. [Part 3] Do most people like to share good news with others?
13. [Part 3] What kind of good news do people often share in the community?
14. [Part 3] How does social media help people access information?
15. [Part 3] Should the media only publish good news?
16. [Part 3] Is it good to share something on social media?

## 682. 常用网站【海外】 / 事物 / HIDDEN
1. [Part 2] Describe a website you often visit You should say: How you found ou about it What it is about How often you visit it And explain why you often visit it
2. [Part 3] What are the differences between old people and young people when they use the internet?
3. [Part 3] What kind of people still go to the library to read and study?
4. [Part 3] Are libraeies still necessary? Why?
5. [Part 3] Why do some people like to read the news on the internet instead of getting it from TV?
6. [Part 3] What's the difference between the internet and television?
7. [Part 3] What are the most popular and least popular apps in China?
8. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What are some of the different reasons why people use the Internet?
9. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Some people say that different age groups have different tastes on Internet content. What do you think?
10. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What influence can (or, does) the Internet have on children? And what about teenagers?
11. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Do you think parents should control what Internet sites their children visit on the Internet?
12. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What do you think of people who have a computer and what do you think of those who don’t have one?
13. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] Compare the types of people who don’t use the Internet with those who do.
14. [Part 3 / HIDDEN] What (kinds of ) people don’t use the Internet and what are the disadvantages that these people suffer because they don’t use the Internet?
